15 Aug 2016 17:10:46 : LimitlessMc, mainchat, Gilles#3169, @Jay113355  @Staff you maybe have no way to solve this, but when your game crashes or you disconnect a few seconds (maybe longer idk) after you swap pokemon from party and pc, the pc saves but the party doesnt. this made me (and many others) to lose pokemon. The pokemon in the party will be the same like they were before using the PC, but the PC did save the changes. This is one of the reasons people get dupes/copies of pokemon they already have, wich are able to replace pokemon that were in the pc. Im not sure if it is possible to do anything about it, but i tought it would a good idea to tell.
